<script type='text/javascript'>
window.fbAsyncInit = function() {

    FB.init({
                 appId      : '411295799005740',
                 cookie     : true,
                 xfbml      : true,
                 version    : 'v2.12',
                 status     : 0
        });

     console.log("FB.init v2.12");

      FB.getLoginStatus(function(response) {
            if (response.status === 'connected') {
                  // Logged into your app and Facebook.
               console.log('Connected : ' +JSON.stringify(response));

            // since new API 2.4 need 
           // docasne email pryc ,email,
           FB.api('/me?fields=id,locale', function(res) {
           console.log('Successful FB login id: ' + res.id ); 

           $("#facebookID").val(  res.id  );

            var lang="pl";
 ;
	    var url="fbconfirm.php?fbid=" + res.id + "&lang=" + lang    ;

	     if(  typeof res.email === 'undefined' ) {   
        	     console.error('sorry no facebook email');
	     }
	     else {
                console.log('facebook email: ' + res.email );
                 url= url + "&email=" +   res.email ; 
             }
             console.log('URL: ' + url );

             $.getJSON(url, function(data){
                       console.log("get json data : " +  JSON.stringify(data)  );
                       var email = ""
                       var azuid =   data.azuid;
                       $("#emailID").val(   azuid );

                       if(  typeof data.email === 'undefined' )  email = "azuid:" + azuid ; // anonympus
                       else email = data.email;

                       $("#email").val(  email  );

                 } );




          });

        } else  console.log('Not connected to FB');

      });



   };


  (function(d, s, id){
     var js, fjs = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
     if (d.getElementById(id)) {return;}
     js = d.createElement(s); js.id = id;
     js.src = "//connect.facebook.net/pl_PL/all.js";
     fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js, fjs);
   }(document, 'script', 'facebook-jssdk'));


function PostToFacebook( tweetText , url )
{
        var  ajaxUrl  =  'getShortLink.php?url=' + url;
         // zkus udelat short url
         $.ajax({
            url:  ajaxUrl ,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function(obj) { 
              if( obj.status_code == 200 ) { 
                  FB.ui({
                          method: 'feed',
                          link:    obj.surl ,
                          caption: tweetText ,
                   }, function(response){ });
               }
             },
             async:false
            });


}
</script>
